       IDENTIFICATION DIVISION.                                                 
       PROGRAM-ID.    BP13C39C.

      * ========================================================== *            
      * SYSTEM OF COMMITMENT (BP13)                                *            
      * ========================================================== *            
      *                                                            *            
      *    OBJECTIVE  :                                            *            
      *        1.  THIS PROGRAMME WILL CREATE THE GL DETAIL        *            
      *            TRANSACTION FILE BP13F180 FOR THE VARIOUS       *            
      *            FEES RAISED AND RECEIVED ON A MONTHLY BASIS.    *            
      *            (FOR LBS AND FLEXI CASES)                       *            
      *     INPUT FILES:  1. BP13F120                              *            
      *                   2. BP13K690 - FOR GRANTS                 *            
      *     OUTPUT FILES: 1. BP13F180                              *            
      *     LISTING:      1. BP13L39C (CONTROL LIST)               *            
      *                                                            *            
      * ---------------------------------------------------------- *            
      * CHG-NO   BY   DATE     DESCRIPTION                         *            
      * -------  ---  ------   -----------                         *            
      * BP135903 FNP1 02112015  NEW PGM (SIMILAR TO BP13C395)      *            
      * BP135903 FNP1 17032016  REPLACED VR WITH SA IN F180-JR-SC  *            
      * BP136398 FNP1 26052016  CATER FOR AMORTISATION OF GRANTS AND            
      *                         PREMIUM                            *            
      * BP136965 FNP1 25082017  INCLUDE ACCUM IN COMPUTING FOR AMT *            
      *                         FOR SRG FOR TRANS = 38             *            
      * BP137219 FNP1 21032018  CATER FOR FSH GRANT/SALES PRICE    *            
      * BP137181 FNP1 29062018  CHANGE 'FS' TO 'SE' FOR F180-JR-SC *            
      * BP138083 KR13 18012020  ADDED EHG                          *            
      * BP138560 FP6  28122020  ADDED LHG AND EXPAND TO 5-ROOM     *            
      * BP138663 FP6  28062021  CATER FOR AMORTISATION OF CCA FLAT *            
      * BP138944 FP6  14102021  EXPAND K690 FROM 600 TO 800        *            
      *                         ADDED SUG                          *            
      * BP139942 ZAR7 21032024  REPALCE 410101 WITH 41CZ01         *            
      * ********************************************************** *            
                                                                                
       ENVIRONMENT DIVISION.                                                    
       CONFIGURATION SECTION.                                                   
       SOURCE-COMPUTER. IBM-4341.                                               
       OBJECT-COMPUTER. IBM-4341.                                               
                                                                                
       INPUT-OUTPUT SECTION.                                                    
       FILE-CONTROL.                                                            
                                                                                
           SELECT BP13F120 ASSIGN TO  BP13F120.                                 
                                                                                
           SELECT SY02F001 ASSIGN TO  SY02F001.                                 
                                                                                
           SELECT BP13F180 ASSIGN TO BP13F180.                                  
                                                                                
           SELECT BP13K690 ASSIGN       TO BP13K690                             
                           ACCESS MODE  IS DYNAMIC                              
                           ORGANIZATION IS INDEXED                              
                           RECORD KEY   IS K690-KEY-FLD                         
                           FILE STATUS  IS K690-STATUS.                         
                                                                                
           SELECT BP13L39C ASSIGN TO BP13L39C.                                  
                                                                                
                                                                                
       DATA DIVISION.                                                           
       FILE SECTION.                                                            
                                                                                
       FD  BP13F120                                                             
           BLOCK CONTAINS 0 RECORDS                                             
           RECORD CONTAINS 150 CHARACTERS                                       
           RECORDING MODE F                                                     
           LABEL RECORDS ARE STANDARD.                                          
       COPY BP13F120.                                                           
                                                                                
       FD  BP13F180                                                             
           BLOCK CONTAINS 0 RECORDS                                             
           RECORD CONTAINS 120 CHARACTERS                                       
           RECORDING MODE F                                                     
           LABEL RECORDS ARE OMITTED.                                           
       COPY BP13F180.                                                           
                                                                                
       FD  BP13K690                                                             
           RECORD CONTAINS 800 CHARACTERS.                                      
       COPY BP13K690.                                                           
                                                                                
       FD BP13L39C                                                              
           BLOCK CONTAINS 0 RECORDS                                             
           RECORD CONTAINS 132 CHARACTERS                                       
           LABEL RECORDS ARE OMITTED                                            
           RECORDING MODE F                                                     
           DATA RECORD IS BP13L39C-REPORT.                                      
       01  BP13L39C-REPORT               PIC X(132).                            
                                                                                
       COPY SY02F001.

       PROCEDURE DIVISION.                                                      
                                                                                
       000-MAINT-ROUTINE.                                                       
                                                                                
           PERFORM 100-OPEN-FILE             THRU 100-EXIT.                     
           PERFORM 200-READ-F120             THRU 200-EXIT.                     
           PERFORM 300-PROCESS-GLTRAN-DETAIL THRU 300-EXIT                      
                   UNTIL WS-F120-EOF-FLAG = 'Y'.                                
           PERFORM 700-PRINT-REPORT          THRU 700-EXIT.                     
           PERFORM 999-CLOSE-FILES           THRU 999-EXIT.                     
                                                                                
       000-EXIT.                                                                
           EXIT.                                                                
                                                                                
      ***************************************************************           
      *    OPENING FILES SECTION                                    *           
      ***************************************************************           
       100-OPEN-FILE.                                                           
           OPEN INPUT BP13F120                                                  
                      BP13K690                                                  
                      SY02F001                                                  
               OUTPUT BP13F180                                                  
                      BP13L39C.                                                 
                                                                                
           IF K690-STATUS NOT = 00 AND 97                                       
              MOVE K690-STATUS          TO RETURN-CODE                          
              DISPLAY 'ERROR OPENING BM06K690 FILE ' K690-STATUS                
              GO TO 999-CLOSE-FILES.                                            
                                                                                
           READ SY02F001 AT END MOVE 'Y' TO SY02F001-EOF.                       
           IF SY02F001-EOF = 'Y'                                                
              DISPLAY 'RECORD NOT FOUND IN SY02F001.'                           
              DISPLAY 'PROCESSING TERMINATED.'                                  
              PERFORM 999-CLOSE-FILES                                           
           ELSE                                                                 
              MOVE F001-DTE-CURRENT TO WS-F180-TRANS-DATE                       
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
       100-EXIT.                                                                
           EXIT.                                                                
                                                                                
      *****************************************************************         
      *    READ FILE BP13F120 FROM THE BEGINING                       *         
      *****************************************************************         
       200-READ-F120.                                                           
                                                                                
           READ BP13F120  AT END                                                
                MOVE 'Y' TO WS-F120-EOF-FLAG                                    
                GO TO 200-EXIT.                                                 
           PERFORM 600-CHK-PERIOD    THRU 600-EXIT.                             
           PERFORM 610-CHK-TRAN-DTE  THRU 610-EXIT.                             
           ADD 1 TO WS-READ-F120-COUNT.                                         
                                                                                
       200-EXIT.                                                                
           EXIT.                                                                
                                                                                
                                                                                
      ******************************************************************        
      *    CHECKS FOR THE PAYMENT TYPE AND TRANSFER CONTROL TO CHECK   *        
      *    FOR TRANSACTION TYPE.                                       *        
      ******************************************************************        
       300-PROCESS-GLTRAN-DETAIL.                                               
                                                                                
           MOVE SPACES TO WS-NUM-BACKDATE.                                      
           PERFORM 330-READ-BP13K690   THRU 330-EXIT.                           
           PERFORM 310-PROCESS-REG-FEE THRU 310-EXIT.                           
                                                                                
           PERFORM 200-READ-F120          THRU 200-EXIT.                        
                                                                                
       300-EXIT.                                                                
           EXIT.                                                                
      *************************************************************             
      *    CHECKING FOR TRANSACTION TYPE FOR                      *             
      *    CDE-TRANS-TYPE = 37                                    *             
      *    CDE-TRANS-TYPE = 38 - REVERSAL                         *             
      *************************************************************             
       310-PROCESS-REG-FEE.                                                     
                                                                                
           EVALUATE TRUE                                                        
              WHEN F120-CDE-TRANS-TYPE = '37'                                   
                 PERFORM 400-DR-DEFER          THRU 400-EXIT                    
                 PERFORM 500-CR-AMORT          THRU 500-EXIT                    
                 IF WS-K690-FOUND = 'Y'                                         
                    PERFORM 410-DR-GRANT-PREM  THRU 410-EXIT                    
                    PERFORM 510-CR-AMORT-OTHER THRU 510-EXIT                    
                 END-IF                                                         
              WHEN F120-CDE-TRANS-TYPE = '38'                                   
                 PERFORM 401-CR-DEFER          THRU 401-EXIT                    
                 PERFORM 501-DR-AMORT          THRU 501-EXIT                    
                 IF WS-K690-FOUND = 'Y'                                         
                    PERFORM 410-DR-GRANT-PREM  THRU 410-EXIT                    
                    PERFORM 510-CR-AMORT-OTHER THRU 510-EXIT                    
      *             PERFORM 420-CR-GRANT-PREM  THRU 420-EXIT                    
      *             PERFORM 520-DR-AMORT-OTHER THRU 520-EXIT                    
                 END-IF                                                         
           END-EVALUATE.                                                        
                                                                                
       310-EXIT.                                                                
           EXIT.                                                                
                                                                                
      ******************************************************************        
      *    READ BP13K690 TO GET THE AMORT AMOUNT FOR GRANT AND FOR     *        
      *    PREMIUM                                                     *        
      ******************************************************************        
       330-READ-BP13K690.                                                       
                                                                                
           MOVE SPACES            TO K690-KEY-FLD.                              
           MOVE F120-NUM-SCH-ACCT TO K690-KEY-FLD.                              
                                                                                
           READ BP13K690.                                                       
                                                                                
           EVALUATE K690-STATUS                                                 
             WHEN 00                                                            
                MOVE 'Y' TO WS-K690-FOUND                                       
                ADD 1 TO K690-FND-CNT                                           
                PERFORM 340-INITIALIZE-FIELDS    THRU 340-EXIT                  
             WHEN 23                                                            
                MOVE 'N' TO WS-K690-FOUND                                       
                ADD 1 TO K690-NFND-CNT                                          
                MOVE SPACES TO K690-REC                                         
                INITIALIZE K690-REC                                             
             WHEN OTHER                                                         
                DISPLAY 'BP13K690 READ ERROR, STATUS IS '                       
                       K690-STATUS ' KEY IS ' K690-KEY-FLD                      
                       MOVE K690-STATUS TO RETURN-CODE                          
                PERFORM 999-CLOSE-FILES  THRU 999-EXIT                          
           END-EVALUATE.                                                        
                                                                                
       330-EXIT.                                                                
           EXIT.                                                                
                                                                                
       340-INITIALIZE-FIELDS.                                                   
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-INCOME-ACCUM > K690-AMT-AMORT-INCOME-MTH           
              IF F120-AMT-RECEIPT = K690-AMT-AMORT-INCOME-ACCUM                 
                 MOVE 'Y' TO WS-NUM-BACKDATE                                    
              END-IF                                                            
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-SINGLES-PREMIUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-SINGLES-PREMIUM                           
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-MTH NOT NUMERIC                                
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-MTH                             
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM                           
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-SC-SPR-PREMIUM  NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-SC-SPR-PREMIUM                            
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-SPR-MTH   NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-SPR-MTH                             
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-SPR-ACCUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-SPR-ACCUM                           
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-ELDERLY-PREMIUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-ELDERLY-PREMIUM                           
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-ELD-MTH   NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-ELD-MTH                             
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-ELD-ACCUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-ELD-ACCUM                           
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AHG-GRANT       NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AHG-GRANT                                 
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-AHG-MTH   NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-AHG-MTH                             
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-AHG-ACCUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-AHG-ACCUM                           
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-EHG-GRANT       NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-EHG-GRANT                                 
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-EHG-MTH   NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-EHG-MTH                             
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-EHG-ACCUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-EHG-ACCUM                           
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-LHG-GRANT       NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-LHG-GRANT                                 
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-LHG-MTH   NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-LHG-MTH                             
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-LHG-ACCUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-LHG-ACCUM                           
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-SHG-GRANT       NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-SHG-GRANT                                 
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-SHG-MTH   NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-SHG-MTH                             
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-SHG-ACCUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-SHG-ACCUM                           
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-SRG-GRANT       NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-SRG-GRANT                                 
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-SRG-MTH   NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-SRG-MTH                             
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-SRG-ACCUM NOT NUMERIC                              
              MOVE ZEROES TO K690-AMT-AMORT-SRG-ACCUM                           
           END-IF.

           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-AMORT-REG-ACCUM NOT NUMERIC

           END-IF.

      *****************************************************************         
      *    DEFERRED INCOME - SALES PROCEEDS FROM UNITS SOLD BY SOS              
      *****************************************************************         
       400-DR-DEFER.                                                            
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-FSG-GRANT NOT = ZEROES                                   
                                                                                
              MOVE SPACES              TO   F180-GL-REC                         
              MOVE ZEROES              TO   F180-AMT-GST-RATE                   
              MOVE 'SE'                TO   F180-JR-SC                          
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-YY    TO   F180-JR-YY F180-TRANS-YY            
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-MM    TO   F180-JR-MM F180-TRANS-MM            
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-DD    TO   F180-TRANS-DD                       
              MOVE WS-F180-PERIOD      TO   F180-PERIOD                         
              MOVE F120-NUM-SCH-ACCT   TO   F180-NUM-SCH-ACC                    
              MOVE 'FSH'               TO   F180-DTE-POST                       
              COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = F120-AMT-RECEIPT                            
                                                                                
              MOVE SPACES              TO   WS-ACC-NO1                          
              MOVE '0'                 TO   WS-ACC-LEAD                         
              MOVE '57'                TO   WS-ACC-FILLER                       
              MOVE '419200'            TO   WS-ACC-INTERNAL                     
              MOVE '4045'              TO   WS-ACC-GL                           
              MOVE 'DEFERRED INCOME FSH SALES PRICE'                            
                                       TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                     
              ADD   1                  TO   WS-DR-DEFER-FSH-SP                  
              ADD F180-CR-AMT          TO   WS-DR-DEFER-AMT-FSH-SP              
              MOVE WS-ACC-NO1          TO   WS-DEFER-GL-FSH-SP                  
                                            F180-ACC-NO1                        
              WRITE F180-GL-REC                                                 
              ADD 1                    TO   WS-WRITE-F180-COUNT                 
                                                                                
           ELSE                                                                 
              MOVE SPACES              TO   F180-GL-REC                         
              MOVE ZEROES              TO   F180-AMT-GST-RATE                   
              MOVE 'SF'                TO   F180-JR-SC                          
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-YY    TO   F180-JR-YY F180-TRANS-YY            
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-MM    TO   F180-JR-MM F180-TRANS-MM            
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-DD    TO   F180-TRANS-DD                       
              MOVE WS-F180-PERIOD      TO   F180-PERIOD                         
              MOVE F120-NUM-SCH-ACCT   TO   F180-NUM-SCH-ACC                    
              IF K690-CDE-TYP-ACTUSE = '01' AND                                 
                 K690-CDE-MODL-DESG  = '74'                                     
                 MOVE 'CCA'               TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
                 COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = F120-AMT-RECEIPT                         
                                                                                
                 MOVE SPACES              TO   WS-ACC-NO1                       
                 MOVE '0'                 TO   WS-ACC-LEAD                      
                 MOVE '57'                TO   WS-ACC-FILLER                    
                 MOVE '407600'            TO   WS-ACC-INTERNAL                  
                 MOVE '4046'              TO   WS-ACC-GL                        
                 MOVE 'DEFERRED INCOME SHORT LEASE CCA'                         
                                          TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                  
                 ADD   1                  TO   WS-DR-DEFER-LB-CCA               
                 ADD F180-CR-AMT          TO   WS-DR-DEFER-AMT-LB-CCA           
                 MOVE WS-ACC-NO1          TO   WS-DEFER-GL-LB-CCA               
                                               F180-ACC-NO1                     
              ELSE                                                              
                 MOVE 'FLX'               TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
                 COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = F120-AMT-RECEIPT                         
                                                                                
                 MOVE SPACES              TO   WS-ACC-NO1                       
                 MOVE '0'                 TO   WS-ACC-LEAD                      
                 MOVE '57'                TO   WS-ACC-FILLER                    
                 MOVE '407600'            TO   WS-ACC-INTERNAL                  
                 MOVE '4041'              TO   WS-ACC-GL                        
                 MOVE 'DEFERRED INCOME SHORT LEASE'                             
                                          TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                  
                 ADD   1                  TO   WS-DR-DEFER-LB                   
                 ADD F180-CR-AMT          TO   WS-DR-DEFER-AMT-LB               
                 MOVE WS-ACC-NO1          TO   WS-DEFER-GL-LB                   
                                               F180-ACC-NO1                     
              END-IF                                                            
              WRITE F180-GL-REC                                                 
              ADD 1                    TO   WS-WRITE-F180-COUNT                 
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
       400-EXIT.                                                                
           EXIT.

      *****************************************************************         
      *    SC/SPR, ELD, SINGLES PREM/ AHG, EHG, SHG, SRG, REG GRANT             
      *****************************************************************         
       410-DR-GRANT-PREM.                                                       
                                                                                
      ***SINGLES PREMIUM                                                        
           IF K690-AMT-SINGLES-PREMIUM NOT = ZEROES                             
              MOVE SPACES              TO   F180-GL-REC                         
              MOVE ZEROES              TO   F180-AMT-GST-RATE                   
              MOVE 'SF'                TO   F180-JR-SC                          
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-YY    TO   F180-JR-YY F180-TRANS-YY            
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-MM    TO   F180-JR-MM F180-TRANS-MM            
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-DD    TO   F180-TRANS-DD                       
              MOVE WS-F180-PERIOD      TO   F180-PERIOD                         
              MOVE F120-NUM-SCH-ACCT   TO   F180-NUM-SCH-ACC                    
              IF K690-CDE-TYP-ACTUSE = '01' AND                                 
                 K690-CDE-MODL-DESG  = '74'                                     
                 MOVE 'CCA-SGP'           TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
                 IF WS-NUM-BACKDATE = 'Y'                                       
                    COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM              
                 ELSE                                                           
                    IF F120-CDE-TRANS-TYPE = '38'                               
                       COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = K690-AMT-SINGLES-PREMIUM -         
                                             K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM           
                    ELSE                                                        
                       COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-MTH             
                    END-IF                                                      
                 END-IF                                                         
                                                                                
                 MOVE SPACES              TO   WS-ACC-NO1                       
                 MOVE '0'                 TO   WS-ACC-LEAD                      
                 MOVE '57'                TO   WS-ACC-FILLER                    
                 MOVE '41CZ01'            TO   WS-ACC-INTERNAL                  
                 MOVE '4046'              TO   WS-ACC-GL                        
                 MOVE 'SINGLES PREMIUM SHORT LEASE CCA'                         
                                          TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                  
                 ADD   1                  TO   WS-DR-SGP-CCA                    
                 ADD F180-CR-AMT          TO   WS-DR-SGP-AMT-CCA                
                 MOVE WS-ACC-NO1          TO   WS-SGP-GL-CCA                    
                                               F180-ACC-NO1                     
              ELSE                                                              
                 MOVE 'SGP'               TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
                 IF WS-NUM-BACKDATE = 'Y'                                       
                    COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM              
                 ELSE                                                           
                    IF F120-CDE-TRANS-TYPE = '38'                               
                       COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = K690-AMT-SINGLES-PREMIUM -         
                                             K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM           
                    ELSE                                                        
                       COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-MTH             
                    END-IF                                                      
                 END-IF                                                         
                                                                                
                 MOVE SPACES              TO   WS-ACC-NO1                       
                 MOVE '0'                 TO   WS-ACC-LEAD                      
                 MOVE '57'                TO   WS-ACC-FILLER                    
                 MOVE '41CZ01'            TO   WS-ACC-INTERNAL                  
                 MOVE '4041'              TO   WS-ACC-GL                        
                 MOVE 'SINGLES PREMIUM SHORT LEASE'                             
                                          TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                  
                 ADD   1                  TO   WS-DR-SGP                        
                 ADD F180-CR-AMT          TO   WS-DR-SGP-AMT                    
                 MOVE WS-ACC-NO1          TO   WS-SGP-GL                        
                                               F180-ACC-NO1                     
              END-IF                                                            
              WRITE F180-GL-REC                                                 
              ADD 1                    TO   WS-WRITE-F180-COUNT                 
           END-IF.

      ***AHG GRANT                                                              
           IF K690-AMT-AHG-GRANT       NOT = ZEROES                             
              MOVE SPACES              TO   F180-GL-REC                         
              MOVE ZEROES              TO   F180-AMT-GST-RATE                   
              MOVE 'SF'                TO   F180-JR-SC                          
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-YY    TO   F180-JR-YY F180-TRANS-YY            
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-MM    TO   F180-JR-MM F180-TRANS-MM            
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-DD    TO   F180-TRANS-DD                       
              MOVE WS-F180-PERIOD      TO   F180-PERIOD                         
              MOVE F120-NUM-SCH-ACCT   TO   F180-NUM-SCH-ACC                    
              MOVE 'AHG'               TO   F180-DTE-POST                       
              IF WS-NUM-BACKDATE = 'Y'                                          
                 COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = K690-AMT-AMORT-AHG-ACCUM                 
              ELSE                                                              
                 IF F120-CDE-TRANS-TYPE = '38'                                  
                    COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = K690-AMT-AHG-GRANT       -            
                                          K690-AMT-AMORT-AHG-ACCUM              
                 ELSE                                                           
                    COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = K690-AMT-AMORT-AHG-MTH                
                 END-IF                                                         
              END-IF                                                            
                                                                                
              MOVE SPACES              TO   WS-ACC-NO1                          
              MOVE '9'                 TO   WS-ACC-LEAD                         
              MOVE '57'                TO   WS-ACC-FILLER                       
              MOVE '407000'            TO   WS-ACC-INTERNAL                     
              EVALUATE K690-CDE-TYP-ACTUSE                                      
                WHEN '01'                                                       
                  MOVE '5051'          TO   WS-ACC-GL                           
                  MOVE 'SOC-AMORT AHG GRANT OF 1RM SHORT LEASE'                 
                                       TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                     
                  ADD   1              TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AHG-1RM                 
                  ADD F180-CR-AMT      TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AMT-AHG-1RM             
                  MOVE WS-ACC-NO1      TO   WS-GL-AHG-1RM                       
                                            F180-ACC-NO1                        
                WHEN '02'                                                       
                  MOVE '5053'          TO   WS-ACC-GL                           
                  MOVE 'SOC-AMORT AHG GRANT OF 2RM SHORT LEASE'                 
                                       TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                     
                  ADD   1              TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AHG-2RM                 
                  ADD F180-CR-AMT      TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AMT-AHG-2RM             
                  MOVE WS-ACC-NO1      TO   WS-GL-AHG-2RM                       
                                            F180-ACC-NO1                        
                WHEN '03'                                                       
                  MOVE '5054'          TO   WS-ACC-GL                           
                  MOVE 'SOC-AMORT AHG GRANT OF 3RM SHORT LEASE'                 
                                       TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                     
                  ADD   1              TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AHG-3RM                 
                  ADD F180-CR-AMT      TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AMT-AHG-3RM             
                  MOVE WS-ACC-NO1      TO   WS-GL-AHG-3RM                       
                                            F180-ACC-NO1                        
                WHEN '04'                                                       
                  MOVE '5055'          TO   WS-ACC-GL                           
                  MOVE 'SOC-AMORT AHG GRANT OF 4RM SHORT LEASE'                 
                                       TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                     
                  ADD   1              TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AHG-4RM                 
                  ADD F180-CR-AMT      TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AMT-AHG-4RM             
                  MOVE WS-ACC-NO1      TO   WS-GL-AHG-4RM                       
                                            F180-ACC-NO1                        
                WHEN '05'                                                       
                  MOVE '5056'          TO   WS-ACC-GL                           
                  MOVE 'SOC-AMORT AHG GRANT OF 5RM SHORT LEASE'                 
                                       TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                     
                  ADD   1              TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AHG-5RM                 
                  ADD F180-CR-AMT      TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AMT-AHG-5RM             
                  MOVE WS-ACC-NO1      TO   WS-GL-AHG-5RM                       
                                            F180-ACC-NO1                        
                WHEN '06'                                                       
                WHEN '08'                                                       
                  MOVE '5058'          TO   WS-ACC-GL                           
                  MOVE 'SOC-AMORT AHG GRANT OF EX/MG SHORT LEASE'               
                                       TO   F180-TRANS-DESC                     
                  ADD   1              TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AHG-6RM                 
                  ADD F180-CR-AMT      TO   WS-DR-AMORT-AMT-AHG-6RM             
                  MOVE WS-ACC-NO1      TO   WS-GL-AHG-6RM                       
                                            F180-ACC-NO1                        
              END-EVALUATE                                                      
                                                                                
              WRITE F180-GL-REC                                                 
              ADD 1                    TO   WS-WRITE-F180-COUNT                 
           END-IF.

      ***SINGLES PREMIUM                                                        
           IF K690-AMT-SINGLES-PREMIUM NOT = ZEROES                             
              MOVE SPACES              TO   F180-GL-REC                         
              MOVE ZEROES              TO   F180-AMT-GST-RATE                   
              MOVE 'SF'                TO   F180-JR-SC                          
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-YY    TO   F180-JR-YY F180-TRANS-YY

              MOVE WS-F180-PERIOD      TO   F180-PERIOD                         
              MOVE F120-NUM-SCH-ACCT   TO   F180-NUM-SCH-ACC                    
              IF K690-CDE-TYP-ACTUSE = '01' AND                                 
                 K690-CDE-MODL-DESG  = '74'                                     
                 MOVE 'CCA-SGP'           TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
                 IF WS-NUM-BACKDATE = 'Y'                                       
                    MOVE K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM TO F180-CR-AMT                
                 ELSE                                                           
                    MOVE K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-MTH   TO F180-CR-AMT                
                 END-IF                                                         
                                                                                
                 MOVE SPACES              TO   WS-ACC-NO1                       
                 MOVE '0'                 TO   WS-ACC-LEAD                      
                 MOVE '57'                TO   WS-ACC-FILLER                    
                 MOVE '41CZ01'            TO   WS-ACC-INTERNAL                  
                 MOVE '4046'              TO   WS-ACC-GL

                 MOVE WS-ACC-NO1          TO   WS-SGP-GL-CCA                    
                                               F180-ACC-NO1                     
              ELSE                                                              
                 MOVE 'SGP'               TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
                 IF WS-NUM-BACKDATE = 'Y'                                       
                    MOVE K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM TO F180-CR-AMT                
                 ELSE                                                           
                    MOVE K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-MTH   TO F180-CR-AMT                
                 END-IF                                                         
                                                                                
                 MOVE SPACES              TO   WS-ACC-NO1                       
                 MOVE '0'                 TO   WS-ACC-LEAD                      
                 MOVE '57'                TO   WS-ACC-FILLER                    
                 MOVE '41CZ01'            TO   WS-ACC-INTERNAL                  
                    MOVE '4041'           TO   WS-ACC-GL                        
                 MOVE 'SINGLES PREMIUM SHORT LEASE'                             
                                          TO   F180-TRANS-DESC

                 MOVE WS-ACC-NO1          TO   WS-SGP-GL

           END-IF.

       500-CR-AMORT.                                                            
                                                                                
           IF K690-AMT-FSG-GRANT       NOT = ZEROES                             
              MOVE SPACES                 TO   F180-GL-REC                      
              MOVE ZEROES                 TO   F180-AMT-GST-RATE                
              MOVE 'SE'                   TO   F180-JR-SC                       
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-YY       TO   F180-JR-YY F180-TRANS-YY         
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-MM       TO   F180-JR-MM F180-TRANS-MM         
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-DD       TO   F180-TRANS-DD                    
              MOVE WS-F180-PERIOD         TO   F180-PERIOD                      
              MOVE F120-NUM-SCH-ACCT      TO   F180-NUM-SCH-ACC                 
              MOVE 'FSH'                  TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
              COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = 0 - F120-AMT-RECEIPT                        
                                                                                
              MOVE SPACES                 TO WS-ACC-NO1                         
              MOVE '9'                    TO WS-ACC-LEAD                        
              MOVE '57'                   TO WS-ACC-FILLER                      
              MOVE '5057'                 TO WS-ACC-GL                          
              MOVE '419200'               TO WS-ACC-INTERNAL                    
              MOVE 'SOC-AMORT INCOME OF FSH SALES PRICE'                        
                                          TO F180-TRANS-DESC

                                             F180-ACC-NO1                       
                                                                                
              WRITE F180-GL-REC                                                 
              ADD 1                       TO   WS-WRITE-F180-COUNT              
                                                                                
           ELSE                                                                 
              MOVE SPACES                 TO   F180-GL-REC                      
              MOVE ZEROES                 TO   F180-AMT-GST-RATE                
              MOVE 'SF'                   TO   F180-JR-SC                       
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-YY       TO   F180-JR-YY F180-TRANS-YY         
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-MM       TO   F180-JR-MM F180-TRANS-MM         
              MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-DD       TO   F180-TRANS-DD                    
              MOVE WS-F180-PERIOD         TO   F180-PERIOD                      
              MOVE F120-NUM-SCH-ACCT      TO   F180-NUM-SCH-ACC                 
                                                                                
              COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = 0 - F120-AMT-RECEIPT                        
                                                                                
              MOVE SPACES                 TO WS-ACC-NO1                         
              MOVE '9'                    TO WS-ACC-LEAD                        
              MOVE '57'                   TO WS-ACC-FILLER                      
                                                                                
              EVALUATE K690-CDE-TYP-ACTUSE                                      
                 WHEN '01'                                                      
                    IF K690-CDE-MODL-DESG  = '74'                               
                       MOVE '5059'           TO WS-ACC-GL                       
                       MOVE '407600'         TO WS-ACC-INTERNAL

                                             TO F180-TRANS-DESC

                       ADD F180-CR-AMT       TO WS-CR-AMORT-AMT-LB-CCA          
                       MOVE WS-ACC-NO1       TO WS-GL-LB-CCA                    
                                                F180-ACC-NO1                    
                       MOVE 'CCA'            TO   F180-DTE-POST                 
                    ELSE                                                        
                       MOVE '5051'           TO WS-ACC-GL                       
                       MOVE '407600'         TO WS-ACC-INTERNAL                 
                       MOVE 'SOC-AMORT INCOME OF 1RM SHORT LEASE'               
                                             TO F180-TRANS-DESC                 
                       ADD   1               TO WS-CR-AMORT-LB-1RM              
                       ADD F180-CR-AMT       TO WS-CR-AMORT-AMT-LB-1RM          
                       MOVE WS-ACC-NO1       TO WS-GL-LB-1RM                    
                                                F180-ACC-NO1                    
                       MOVE 'FLX'            TO   F180-DTE-POST                 
                    END-IF                                                      
                 WHEN '02'                                                      
                    MOVE '5053'           TO WS-ACC-GL                          
                    MOVE '407600'         TO WS-ACC-INTERNAL                    
                    MOVE 'SOC-AMORT INCOME OF 2RM SHORT LEASE'                  
                                          TO F180-TRANS-DESC                    
                    ADD   1               TO WS-CR-AMORT-LB-2RM                 
                    ADD F180-CR-AMT       TO WS-CR-AMORT-AMT-LB-2RM             
                    MOVE WS-ACC-NO1       TO WS-GL-LB-2RM                       
                                             F180-ACC-NO1                       
                    MOVE 'FLX'            TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
                 WHEN '03'                                                      
                    MOVE '5054'           TO WS-ACC-GL                          
                    MOVE '407600'         TO WS-ACC-INTERNAL                    
                    MOVE 'SOC-AMORT INCOME OF 3RM SHORT LEASE'                  
                                          TO F180-TRANS-DESC                    
                    ADD   1               TO WS-CR-AMORT-LB-3RM                 
                    ADD F180-CR-AMT       TO WS-CR-AMORT-AMT-LB-3RM             
                    MOVE WS-ACC-NO1       TO WS-GL-LB-3RM                       
                                             F180-ACC-NO1                       
                    MOVE 'FLX'            TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
                 WHEN '04'                                                      
                    MOVE '5055'           TO WS-ACC-GL                          
                    MOVE '407600'         TO WS-ACC-INTERNAL                    
                    MOVE 'SOC-AMORT INCOME OF 4RM SHORT LEASE'                  
                                          TO F180-TRANS-DESC                    
                    ADD   1               TO WS-CR-AMORT-LB-4RM

                    MOVE 'FLX'            TO   F180-DTE-POST                    
                 WHEN '05'

                 COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = 0 - K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM             
              ELSE

                    COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = 0 -                                   
                                          (K690-AMT-SINGLES-PREMIUM -           
                                           K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-ACCUM)            
                 ELSE                                                           
                    COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = 0 - K690-AMT-AMORT-SGP-MTH            
                 END-IF                                                         
              END-IF                                                            
                                                                                
              MOVE SPACES                 TO WS-ACC-NO1                         
              MOVE '9'                    TO WS-ACC-LEAD                        
              MOVE '57'                   TO WS-ACC-FILLER                      
              MOVE '41CZ01'               TO WS-ACC-INTERNAL

                 WRITE F180-GL-REC                                              
                 ADD 1                       TO   WS-WRITE-F180-COUNT           
              ELSE                                                              
                 MOVE 'REG'                  TO   F180-DTE-POST                 
                 IF WS-NUM-BACKDATE = 'Y'                                       
                    COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = 0 - K690-AMT-AMORT-REG-ACCUM          
                 ELSE                                                           
                    IF F120-CDE-TRANS-TYPE = '38'                               
                       COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = 0 -                                
                                            (K690-AMT-REG-GRANT       -         
                                             K690-AMT-AMORT-REG-ACCUM)          
                    ELSE                                                        
                       COMPUTE F180-CR-AMT = 0 - K690-AMT-AMORT-REG-MTH         
                    END-IF                                                      
                 END-IF                                                         
                                                                                
                 MOVE SPACES                 TO WS-ACC-NO1                      
                 MOVE '0'                    TO WS-ACC-LEAD                     
                 MOVE '57'                   TO WS-ACC-FILLER                   
                 MOVE '419200'               TO WS-ACC-INTERNAL                 
                 MOVE '4041'                 TO WS-ACC-GL                       
                 MOVE 'SOC-AMORT REG GRANT OF SHORT LEASE'                      
                                             TO F180-TRANS-DESC                 
                 ADD   1                     TO WS-CR-REG                       
                 ADD F180-CR-AMT             TO WS-CR-REG-AMT                   
                 MOVE WS-ACC-NO1             TO WS-REG-GL                       
                                                F180-ACC-NO1                    
                 WRITE F180-GL-REC                                              
                 ADD 1                       TO   WS-WRITE-F180-COUNT           
              END-IF                                                            
           END-IF.

      *****************************************************************         
      *    CORRECTING CALENDAR DATE TO FINANCIAL YEAR PERIOD          *         
      *****************************************************************         
       600-CHK-PERIOD.                                                          
                                                                                
                                                                                
           IF WS-F180-TRANS-MM   < 4                                            
              ADD 9  WS-F180-TRANS-MM  GIVING WS-F180-PERIOD.                   
                                                                                
           IF WS-F180-TRANS-MM   > 3                                            
              SUBTRACT 3 FROM WS-F180-TRANS-MM  GIVING WS-F180-PERIOD.          
                                                                                
                                                                                
       600-EXIT.                                                                
           EXIT.                                                                
                                                                                
      ****************************************************************          
      *    MOVING THE APPROPRIATE MONTH END DATE ACCORDING TO        *          
      *    CALENDAR MONTH AND YEAR                                   *          
      ****************************************************************          
       610-CHK-TRAN-DTE.                                                        
           DIVIDE WS-F180-TRANS-CCYY  BY 4 GIVING WS-YEAR REMAINDER             
                                            WS-LEAP-YEAR.                       
                                                                                
           MOVE WS-F180-TRANS-MM TO WS-MONTH.                                   
           IF WS-F180-TRANS-MM = 2                                              
              IF WS-LEAP-YEAR = 0                                               
                 MOVE 29 TO WS-F180-TRANS-DD                                    
              ELSE                                                              
                 MOVE 28 TO WS-F180-TRANS-DD                                    
           ELSE                                                                 
               IF CHECK-MM                                                      
                  MOVE 30 TO WS-F180-TRANS-DD                                   
               ELSE                                                             
                  MOVE 31 TO WS-F180-TRANS-DD.

           EXIT.                                                                
                                                                                
      ***************************************************************           
      *     PRINT REPORT OF RECORDS READ AND WRITTEN TO CLEARING    *           
      *     FILE BP13F120 AND GENERAL LEDGER BP13F180 RESPECTIVELY. *           
      ***************************************************************           
       700-PRINT-REPORT.                                                        
           ADD 1 TO WS-PAGE-COUNT.                                              
                                                                                
           MOVE WS-READ-F120-COUNT    TO L39C-READ-F120-CNT.                    
           MOVE WS-WRITE-F180-COUNT   TO L39C-WRITE-F180-CNT.                   
                                                                                
           MOVE FUNCTION CURRENT-DATE TO WS-CURRENT-DATE.                       
           MOVE CORRESPONDING WS-CURRENT-DATE TO L39C-EDITED-DATE.              
           MOVE WS-PAGE-COUNT                 TO L39C-PAGE.                     
                                                                                
           WRITE BP13L39C-REPORT FROM WS-TITLE-1 AFTER PAGE.                    
           WRITE BP13L39C-REPORT FROM WS-TITLE-2 AFTER 2.                       
           WRITE BP13L39C-REPORT FROM WS-TITLE-3 AFTER 2.                       
           WRITE BP13L39C-REPORT FROM WS-HEADER-LINE-1 AFTER 4.                 
           WRITE BP13L39C-REPORT FROM WS-HEADER-LINE-2 AFTER 2.                 
           WRITE BP13L39C-REPORT FROM WS-SUMMARY-HEADER-1 AFTER 4.              
           WRITE BP13L39C-REPORT FROM WS-SUMMARY-HEADER-2 AFTER 2.              
                                                                                
                                                                                
      **PRINT TOTAL FOR DEFERRED INCOME - LBS/VRL SALES PROCEEDS                
           INITIALIZE WS-SUMMARY-DETAIL-1.                                      
           MOVE WS-DEFER-GL-LB       TO  L39C-DEFER-GL.                         
           MOVE WS-DR-DEFER-LB       TO  L39C-DR-CASES.                         
           MOVE WS-CR-DEFER-LB       TO  L39C-CR-CASES.                         
           MOVE WS-DR-DEFER-AMT-LB   TO  L39C-DR-DEFER-DEBIT.                   
           MOVE WS-CR-DEFER-AMT-LB   TO  L39C-CR-DEFER-CREDIT.                  
           IF L39C-DEFER-GL NOT = SPACES                                        
              WRITE BP13L39C-REPORT FROM WS-SUMMARY-DETAIL-1 AFTER 1            
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
      **PRINT TOTAL FOR DEFERRED INCOME - LBS/VRL SALES PROCEEDS-CCA            
           INITIALIZE WS-SUMMARY-DETAIL-1.                                      
           MOVE WS-DEFER-GL-LB-CCA   TO  L39C-DEFER-GL.                         
           MOVE WS-DR-DEFER-LB-CCA   TO  L39C-DR-CASES.                         
           MOVE WS-CR-DEFER-LB-CCA   TO  L39C-CR-CASES.                         
           MOVE WS-DR-DEFER-AMT-LB-CCA   TO  L39C-DR-DEFER-DEBIT.               
           MOVE WS-CR-DEFER-AMT-LB-CCA   TO  L39C-CR-DEFER-CREDIT.              
           IF L39C-DEFER-GL NOT = SPACES                                        
              WRITE BP13L39C-REPORT FROM WS-SUMMARY-DETAIL-1 AFTER 1            
           END-IF.                                                              
                                                                                
      **PRINT TOTAL FOR DEFERRED INCOME - FSH SALES PRICE                       
           INITIALIZE WS-SUMMARY-DETAIL-1.                                      
           MOVE WS-DEFER-GL-FSH-SP   TO  L39C-DEFER-GL.

      **PRINT TOTAL FOR SINGLES PREMIUM

           MOVE WS-SGP-GL            TO  L39C-DEFER-GL.

      **PRINT TOTAL FOR SC/SPR  PREMIUM
